/*

Original mod by MRN1.

G-SERIES Team mode version

▬▬▬▬▬▬▬▬▬▬▬ஜ۩۞۩ஜ▬▬▬▬▬▬▬▬▬▬▬

Development of this mod started in August 2021.
G stands for "Genocide". It is about "Genocide Super Dreadnought" posted on Discord on April 1, 2021.
The ship featured in this mod is a modern remake of the Genocide Mark 3 Super Dreadnought as a fighter plane.
This mod divides her into her 4 classes. The right is the power system, the left is the speed system, and the center is the balance. The performance difference is not large.
This mod randomly selects maps with dense asteroids and vast spaces carefully selected by MRN1.
All ships in this mod are very fast, so the map size is 150, which is wider than the normal team mode.
Ships with this mod fly very fast, but turn and accelerate poorly.
Ship statuses in this mod are set periodically according to certain laws. Therefore, many ships have stats that are not multiples of 5 other than shield generators.
Aliens appear in this mod. Aliens interfere with your activities.
You can get gems by killing aliens.
This mod uses a "bounce laser". Reflectivity she set to 0.75. Beware of enemy surprise attacks if you are working with two or more ships.
Tier 7 was originally intended to be a space battleship, but was changed to a fighter after completion.

*/

];

this.tick = function(game) {
  if (game.step % 60 === 0)
  {
    var aliens = Math.max(120,Math.min(1,game.ships.length*2));
    if (game.aliens.length<aliens)
    {
      var minute = game.step/3600 ;
      var range = Math.min(alien_types.length,minute/1);
      var index = Math.floor(Math.random()*range);
      var angle = Math.random()*Math.PI*2;
      var alien = alien_types[index] ;
      alien.x = Math.cos(angle)*525 ;
      alien.y = Math.sin(angle)*525 ;
      game.addAlien(alien) ;
    }
    for (var i=0;i<game.ships.length;i++)
    {
      var ship = game.ships[i];
      if (ship.custom.radar_updated === null)
      {
        ship.custom.radar_updated = true ;
        ship.setUIComponent(radar_background);
      }
    }
  }
};
